116479	(Or 3.5)	geworht	Þæt hus hæfdon Romane to ðæm anum tacne *geworht* þæt on swelce healfe swelce hie þonne winnende beon woldan, swa suþ, swa norþ, swa east, swa west, þonne andydan hie þa duru þe on þa healfe open wæs, þæt hie be þæm wiston hwider hie sceoldon. 
116483	(Or 3.5)	betyneda	& þonne hie frið hæfdon, þonne wæron ealle þa dura *betyneda*,

116489	(Or 3.5)	getacnod	On þæm wæs sweotole *getacnod* þæt nan eorþlic man ne mehte swelce lufe & swelce sibbe ofer eallne middangeard gedon swelce þa wæs,

116517	(Or 3.7)	getimbred	Ic sceal hwæðre eft gewendan þæt ic hwelcnehugu dæl gesecge Alexandres dæda; & hu Philippus his fæder IIII hund wintrum æfter þæm þe Romeburg *getimbred* wæs, he feng to Mæcedonia rice on Crecum, & þæt hæfde XXV wintra, & binnan þæm gearum he geeode ealle þa cynericu þe on Crecum wæron.
